<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">

<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid">
<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;5.02.</span></td>
<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On January&#160;9, 2025, the Management Development and Compensation Committee of the Board of Directors of APA Corporation (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Company</span>&#8221;) approved both a new form of Performance Share Program Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Performance Share Program Agreement</span>&#8221;) and a new form of Stock Option Award Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Option Award Agreement</span>,&#8221; and, together with the Performance Share Program Agreement, the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Award Agreements</span>&#8221;). Pursuant to the Award Agreements, the Company will award performance shares (&#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold">Performance Shares</span>&#8221;) and stock options to purchase shares of the Company&#8217;s common stock, respectively, to the Company&#8217;s executive officers under the Company&#8217;s 2016 Omnibus Compensation Plan, as amended. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Performance Share Program Agreement mirrors the Company&#8217;s previous form of performance share program agreement, except that the Performance Share Program Agreement provides that vesting of the Performance Shares is based on two individually weighted measures of performance: Relative Total Shareholder Return (60%) and Cash Return on Invested Capital (40%). </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Option Award Agreement mirrors the Company&#8217;s previous form of stock option award agreement utilized in 2018, with updates based on amendments made to the previously issued stock option award agreements, which include, but are not limited to, revising the definition of &#8220;Involuntary Termination.&#8221; </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The foregoing descriptions of the Award Agreements do not purport to be complete and are subject to, and are qualified in their entirety by, the full text of the Performance Share Program Agreement and the Option Award Agreement, which are attached hereto as Exhibit 10.1 and Exhibit 10.2, respectively, and are incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
<table style="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top" align="left"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;9.01.</span></td>

confirm the number of Conditional Grant RSUs that will actually be awarded as RSUs and the dollar amount of the Conditional Grant Cash Award that will actually be awarded in cash to you based upon measurement of the specific performance goals,
applicable performance percentage levels, and applicable weighting percentages during the Performance Period as set forth in Schedule B to the Agreement, provided that you remain an Eligible Person and employed by the Company or its Affiliate as of
the final day of the Performance Period. Once granted at the conclusion of the Performance Period, such RSUs and the Cash Award shall remain subject to a vesting schedule (as set forth below) (the &#147;<B>Vesting Period</B>&#148;). Once vested, you
shall be paid the value of your RSUs in cash and the cash amount of the Cash Award (in each case, net of cash withheld for applicable tax withholdings) if you remain employed as an Eligible Person during the Vesting Period including the vesting
date.</TD></TR>

Eligible Person at the time of such termination, with (a)&nbsp;vesting of the Target RSUs and (b)&nbsp;vesting of the Target Cash Award, or (ii)&nbsp;on or after a Change of Control which occurs after completion of the Performance Period. Upon such
vesting, the applicable amount of cash, subject to required tax withholding, shall be paid by the Company to you within thirty (30)&nbsp;days of such vesting date.</TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top">If, after the first three (3)&nbsp;months of the Performance Period (and not before), your termination of employment from the Company and the Affiliates occurs by reason of your Retirement, you shall be deemed to continue to be
employed as an Eligible Person for purposes of this Conditional Grant and shall continue to vest with respect to a specified percentage of RSUs and the Cash Award over the Vesting Period, if you meet the Retirement conditions set forth in section 6
of the Agreement. In the event of a Change of Control after you retire during the period commencing on the first day following the first three (3)&nbsp;months of the Performance Period and ending on the last day of the Vesting Period, vesting is
accelerated to 100% for you upon the occurrence of the Change of Control. In the event of a Change of Control prior to your termination of employment by reason of Retirement and after the first three (3)&nbsp;months of the Performance Period and
ending on the last day of the Vesting Period, you shall become 100% vested upon your termination of employment by reason of Retirement. Unless expressly otherwise provided in the Agreement with respect to Retirement and Change of Control, the
applicable amount of cash, subject to required tax withholding, shall be paid by the Company to you upon the earlier to occur of a 409A Change of Control or the normal vesting dates (in the applicable percentage amounts). Payment shall be made
within thirty (30)&nbsp;days of a 409A Change of Control or within sixty (60)&nbsp;days of the normal vesting dates, whichever is applicable.</TD></TR>

on its Stock. Your rights in any such Dividend Equivalents will vest at the same time as, and only to the extent that, the underlying Conditional Grant RSUs or RSUs, as applicable, vest and will be distributed at the same time in cash (subject to
applicable withholdings), and only to the extent, as the related RSUs are</TD></TR>

<TD VALIGN="top"><B>Performance Goals:</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"><B><I>1. Total Shareholder Return</I></B></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top">At the end of the Performance Period, the Committee shall derive and confirm a portion of the number of Conditional Grant RSUs that will actually be awarded as RSUs to you based upon measurement of total shareholder return
(&#147;<B>TSR</B>&#148;) of Stock as compared to a designated Peer Group during the Performance Period, if you remain an Eligible Person and employed by the Company or its Affiliate as of the final day of the Performance Period.</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top">TSR is determined by dividing (i)&nbsp;the sum of the cumulative amount of a company&#146;s or index fund&#146;s dividends for the performance period (assuming <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">same-day</FONT> reinvestment into the
company&#146;s common stock or index fund on the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</FONT> date) and the share price of the company or index fund at the end of the performance period minus the share price at the beginning of the
performance period by (ii)&nbsp;the share price at the beginning of the performance period.</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="8" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>

equivalent on the applicable stock exchange for the three calendar months immediately preceding the beginning of the performance period</P></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="8"></TD>

equivalent on the applicable stock exchange for the last three calendar months of the performance period</P></TD></TR>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>APA Corporation </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>2025 Performance Share Program Agreement </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This 2025 Performance Share Program Agreement (this &#147;<B>Agreement</B>&#148;), dated as of the Grant Date set forth in the Grant Notice, is made between
APA Corporation (together with its Affiliates, the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and the Participant set forth in the Grant Notice. The Grant Notice is included in and made part of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In this Agreement and the Grant Notice, unless the context otherwise requires, words and expressions shall have the meanings given to them in the Plan except
as herein defined. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Definitions </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>409A Change of Control</B>&#148; means a Change of Control that constitutes, with respect to APA Corporation, a &#147;change in the ownership or
effective control of the corporation, or in the ownership of a substantial portion of the assets of the corporation&#148; within the meaning of Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(A)(v) of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the
&#147;<B>Code</B>&#148;) and Treasury Regulations <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Section&nbsp;1.409A-3(i)(5).</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Base Salary</B>&#148;
means, with regard to any Participant, such Participant&#146;s annual base compensation as an employee of the Company determined immediately prior to the beginning of the Performance Period, without regard to any bonus, pension, profit sharing,
stock option, life insurance or salary continuation plan which the Participant either receives or is otherwise entitled to have paid on his or her behalf. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Conditional Grant</B>&#148; means the conditional entitlement, evidenced by this Agreement to receive all or a portion of the Target RSUs and the
Target Cash Award and the Final RSU Amount and Final Cash Award Amount, subject to and in accordance with the provisions of this Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Disability</B>&#148; or &#147;<B>Disabled</B>&#148; means the Participant is unable to engage in any substantial gainful activity by reason of any
medically determinable physical or mental impairment which can be expected to result in death or which has lasted or can be expected to last for a continuous period of not less than 12 months. Participant agrees that a final and binding
determination of &#147;Disability&#148; will be made by the Company&#146;s representative under the Company&#146;s group long-term disability plan or any successor thereto or, if there is no such representative and there is a dispute as to the
determination of &#147;Disability,&#148; it will be decided in a court of law in Harris County, Texas. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Fair Market Value</B>&#148; means the
fair market value of a share of the Stock as determined by the Committee by the reasonable application of such reasonable valuation method, consistently applied, as the Committee deems appropriate; <I>provided, however</I>, that if the Committee has
not made such determination, such fair market value shall be the per share closing price of the Stock as reported on Nasdaq or on such other exchange or electronic trading system as, on the date in question, reports the largest number of traded
shares of stock; <I>provided further, however</I>, that, if there are no Stock transactions on such date, the Fair Market Value shall be determined as of the immediately preceding date on which there were Stock transactions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Final Amount</B>&#148; means with regard to any Participant, the sum of (i)&nbsp;an amount of cash equal to the Fair Market Value of the shares of
Stock underlying the Final RSU Amount and related Dividend Equivalents and (ii)&nbsp;the amount of cash equal to the Final Cash Award Amount. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Final Cash Award Amount</B>&#148; means with regard to any Participant, the Target Cash Award, as specified in each Participant&#146;s Grant Notice,
times the applicable multiple factor determined under the Performance Measures at the end of the Performance Period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Final RSU Amount</B>&#148;
means with regard to any Participant, the number of Target RSUs, as specified in each Participant&#146;s Grant Notice, times the applicable multiple factor determined under the Performance Measures at the end of the Performance Period. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Page 8 of 21 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Grant Notice</B>&#148; means the separate notice, attached as Schedule A hereto, along with
Schedule B, given to the Participant specifying the Target RSUs and Target Cash Award and other applicable performance percentage levels, performance criteria, and applicable weighting percentages for that Participant. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Involuntary Termination</B>&#148; means the termination of employment of the Participant by the Company or its successor or an applicable Affiliate
for any reason on or after a Change of Control; <I>provided</I>, that the termination does not result from an act of the Participant that (a)&nbsp;constitutes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">common-law</FONT> fraud, a felony, or a gross malfeasance
of duty and (b)&nbsp;is materially detrimental to the best interests of the Company or its successor; <I>provided</I> that, notwithstanding anything else in this Agreement to the contrary, an Involuntary Termination shall not be deemed to occur
solely because a Participant transfers employment from the Company to an Affiliate, from an Affiliate to the Company, or from one Affiliate to another Affiliate. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Participant</B>&#148; means an Eligible Person who has been designated to receive one or more Conditional Grants in accordance with the Plan. For
purposes of this Agreement, the group of Eligible Persons shall include all full-time and designated part-time employees of the Company who are employed as employees of the Company (as designated by the Company for payroll purposes), but excluding
Egyptian nationals employed outside of the United States, employees categorized by the Company (for payroll purposes) as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exempt</FONT> support and field staff, leased employees, interns, or any employee of the
Company who is covered under a collective bargaining agreement, unless such collective bargaining agreement specifically provides for coverage under the Plan. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Payout Amount</B>&#148; means the vested portion of the Final Amount. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Peer Group</B>&#148; means the group of companies or index funds selected by the Committee for purposes of this Agreement as set forth in the Grant
Notice. Should consolidation among any Peer Group companies in the marketplace occur during the Performance Period, the Committee will determine the appropriate adjustments to accommodate the reduced number of Peer Group companies for the
Performance Period. Should a Change of Control of APA Corporation occur during the Performance Period, the Committee will determine the appropriate adjustments to measure APA Corporation&#146;s TSR for the Performance Period. The Peer Group
companies for any particular Performance Period shall be determined at the commencement of such Performance Period. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Performance
Measures</B>&#148; means, as set forth in the Grant Notice, (i)&nbsp;APA Corporation&#146;s TSR over the Performance Period compared to the TSR of the Company&#146;s Peer Group over the Performance Period, (ii)&nbsp;APA Corporation&#146;s
achievement of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-established</FONT> performance goals over the Performance Period, or (iii)&nbsp;APA Corporation&#146;s achievement of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-established</FONT> ESG goals over the
Performance Period, as applicable. For purposes of determining TSR performance, at the end of the Performance Period, the Peer Group companies and the Company will be ranked together based on their TSR for the Performance Period from the highest TSR
being number 1 to the lowest TSR being the number of Peer Group companies or index funds, including the Company, remaining in the group at the end of the Performance Period. Based on the Company&#146;s relative TSR rank amongst the Peer Group
companies or index funds for the Performance Period, a Participant who remains employed as of the last day of the Performance Period will be issued RSUs at the close of the Performance Period as determined by the Company&#146;s percentile rank as
set forth in the Grant Notice (the Final Amount). At the end of the Performance Period, the Committee shall also determine and certify the levels of other specific performance goals achieved and apply the applicable performance percentage levels and
weighting percentages as set forth in the Grant Notice. Based on the Company&#146;s level of goal achievement, a Participant who remains employed as of the last day of the Performance Period will be issued RSUs and the Cash Award, as applicable, on
the day following the close of the Performance Period as determined by the Committee as set forth in the Grant Notice (the Final Amount). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Performance Period</B>&#148; means the three-year period as specified in the Grant Notice. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Plan</B>&#148; means the APA Corporation 2016 Omnibus Compensation Plan, as amended. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Retirement</B>&#148; means, with respect to a Participant and for purposes of this Agreement, the
date the Participant terminates employment with the Company after attaining (a)&nbsp;age 55 and (b)&nbsp;a certain combination of age and Years of Service set forth in the Matrix in Exhibit A attached hereto. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Target Cash Award</B>&#148; means, with regard to any Participant, such amount of the Cash Award as specified in each Participant&#146;s Grant
Notice. The amount of such Target Cash Award shall be based upon a target percentage of annual Base Salary determined at the beginning of the Performance Period derived from job level. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Target RSUs</B>&#148; means, with regard to any Participant, such number of RSUs as specified in each Participant&#146;s Grant Notice. The number of
such Target RSUs shall be based upon a target percentage of annual Base Salary determined at the beginning of the Performance Period derived from job level. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Total Shareholder Return</B>&#148; or &#147;<B>TSR</B>&#148; is determined by dividing (i)&nbsp;the sum of the cumulative amount of a company&#146;s
dividends for the Performance Period (assuming <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">same-day</FONT> reinvestment into the company&#146;s common stock on the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</FONT> date) and the share price of the company at
the end of the Performance Period minus the share price at the beginning of the Performance Period, by (ii)&nbsp;the share price at the beginning of the Performance Period. The share price at the beginning of the Performance Period is the average
per share closing price of a share or share equivalent on the applicable stock exchange for the three calendar months immediately preceding the beginning of the Performance Period, and the share price at the end of the Performance Period is the
average per share closing price of a share or share equivalent on the applicable stock exchange for the last three calendar months of the Performance Period. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Voluntary Termination with Cause</B>&#148; occurs upon a Participant&#146;s separation from service of his or her own volition and one or more of the
following conditions occurs without the Participant&#146;s consent on or after a Change of Control: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>(a)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material diminution in the Participant&#146;s base compensation, compared to his or her rate of base
compensation on the date of the Change of Control. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>(b)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material diminution in the Participant&#146;s authority, duties, or responsibilities.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>(c)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material diminution in the authority, duties, or responsibilities of the Participant&#146;s
supervisor, such as a requirement that the Participant (or his or her supervisor) report to a corporate officer or employee instead of reporting directly to the board of directors. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material diminution in the budget over which the Participant retains authority.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material change in the geographic location at which the Participant must perform his or her service,
including, for example the assignment of the Participant to a regular workplace that is more than 50 miles from his or her regular workplace on the date of the Change of Control. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Participant must notify the Company of the existence of one or more adverse conditions specified in clauses (a)&nbsp;through (e) above within 90 days of
the initial existence of the adverse condition. The notice must be provided in writing to the Company or its successor, attention: Head of Human Resources. The notice may be provided by personal delivery or it may be sent by email, inter-office
mail, regular mail (including certified), fax, or any similar method. The Company&#146;s Head of Human Resources or his or her delegate shall acknowledge receipt of the notice within 5 business days; the acknowledgement shall be sent to the
Participant by certified mail. Notwithstanding the foregoing provisions of this definition, if the Company remedies the adverse condition within 30 days of being notified of the adverse condition, no Voluntary Termination with Cause shall occur.

hire by the Company to the date of termination of employment, plus any months required to be recognized under an appropriate acquisition agreement, divided by 12. </P>

each as of the date of the Change of Control. Subject to section 12(b) of this Agreement, payment shall occur within thirty (30)&nbsp;days of a 409A Change of Control <I>provided</I> that if no 409A Change of Control occurs during the Performance
Period, nor during the period of continued vesting as set forth in section 3(b) and 4(c) of this Agreement, then the Final Amount shall be paid by the Company to the Participant who is retired, within sixty (60)&nbsp;days of the vesting dates (in
the applicable percentage amounts) set forth in section 2 of this Agreement, subject to required tax withholding. In the event of a Change of Control prior to the Participant&#146;s termination of employment by reason of Retirement and after the
first three (3)&nbsp;months of the Performance Period and ending on the last day of the Vesting Period, the Participant shall become 100% vested in the unvested Final RSU Amount and the unvested Final Cash Award Amount, each as of the date that the
Participant terminates employment by reason of Retirement. For the purpose of vesting as set forth in the prior sentence, a Participant&#146;s Involuntary Termination or Voluntary Termination with Cause after a Change of Control shall be deemed a
termination by reason of Retirement. Subject to section 12(b) of this Agreement, if the Participant terminates employment by reason of Retirement after a Change of Control, the Participant shall receive payment with respect to 100% of the Final
Amount within sixty (60)&nbsp;days of the vesting dates (in the applicable percentage amounts) as set forth in section 2 of this Agreement, subject to required tax withholding. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

and Years of Service set forth in the Matrix in Exhibit A attached hereto and terminates employment with the Company and the Affiliates by reason of Retirement after the first three (3)&nbsp;months of the Performance Period, it is agreed by the

continued in employment, <I>provided</I> that the Grant Date of the unvested RSUs and the Cash Award is prior to such termination date in an amount of time which allows the Participant to provide the written notice as follows and the Participant has
provided advance written notice not before three (3)&nbsp;months following the Grant Date and not less than the number of months prior to such termination date as set forth in the schedule below to the Company&#146;s Head of Human Resources or his
or her delegate, and to his or her direct manager, regarding the Participant&#146;s intent to terminate employment for reason of Retirement (the period commencing on the first day following the first three (3)&nbsp;months of the Performance Period
and ending on the last day of the Vesting Period being the &#147;<B>Continued Vesting Period</B>&#148;); <I>provided, however</I>, a Participant who is at least age 55 and attained the necessary combination of age and Years of Service under the
Matrix set forth in Exhibit A for Retirement need not provide such advance written notice of his or her intent to terminate employment by reason of Retirement if the Company elects to require such Participant to, or (as part of a reduction in force
or otherwise in writing in exchange for a written release) offers such Participant the opportunity to, terminate employment with the Company by reason of Retirement. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

to comply with, or be exempt from, the applicable requirements of Section&nbsp;409A of the Code and the rules and regulations issued thereunder and shall be administered accordingly. Notwithstanding anything in this Agreement to the contrary, if the
RSUs or Cash Award constitute &#147;deferred compensation&#148; under Section&nbsp;409A of the Code and any RSUs or the Cash Award become payable pursuant to the Participant&#146;s termination of employment, settlement of the RSUs and the Cash Award
shall be delayed for a period of six months after the Participant&#146;s termination of employment if the Participant is a &#147;specified employee&#148; as defined under Code Section&nbsp;409A(a)(2)(B)(i) and if required pursuant to
Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. If settlement of the RSUs and Cash Award is delayed, the RSUs and Cash Award shall be settled on the first day of the first calendar month following the end of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT>
delay period. If the Participant dies during the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">six-month</FONT> delay, the RSUs and Cash Award shall be settled and paid to the Participant&#146;s designated beneficiary, legal representatives, heirs or legatees,
as applicable, as soon as practicable after the date of death. Notwithstanding any provision to the contrary herein, payments made with respect to these Conditional Grants may only be made in a manner and upon an event permitted by Section&nbsp;409A
of the Code, and all payments to be made upon a termination of employment hereunder may only be made upon a &#147;separation from service,&#148; as such term is defined in Section&nbsp;11.1 of the Plan. Participant shall not have any right to
determine a date of payment of any amount under this Agreement. This Agreement may be amended without the consent of the Participant in any respect deemed by the Board or the Committee to be necessary in order to preserve compliance with
Section&nbsp;409A of the Code. If the Conditional Grant and this Agreement is subject to Section&nbsp;409A of the Code and the rules and regulations issued thereunder, and, except as set forth in section 5(a), the vesting date shall be the
&#147;designated payment date&#148; or &#147;specified date&#148; under Treasury Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1.409A-3(d).</FONT> </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

Participant&#146;s assignees shall be addressed to the Administrative Agent, Fidelity, through the Participant&#146;s account at netbenefits.fidelity.com, or such other address as the Company may from time to time specify. All notices to the
Participant shall be addressed to the Participant at the Participant&#146;s address in the Company&#146;s records. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

affect the Participant&#146;s participation in, or benefits under, any other benefit plan or other contract or arrangement maintained by the Company or any Affiliate. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Clawback Policy</B>. If required by the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002 and/or by the Dodd-Frank Wall Street
Reform and Consumer Protection Act of 2010, each Participant&#146;s Award shall be conditioned on repayment or forfeiture in accordance with applicable law. In addition, the Company&#146;s Executive Compensation Clawback Policy is hereby
incorporated by reference and shall form a part of this Agreement and each Participant&#146;s Award shall be subject to such Policy. In connection with an accounting restatement due to the material noncompliance of the Company with any financial
reporting requirement under the U.S. federal securities laws, including any required accounting restatement to correct an error in previously issued financial statements that is material to the previously issued financial statements, or that would
result in a material misstatement if the error were corrected in the current period or left uncorrected in the current period, Awards and payments in connection with Awards granted under this Agreement may be subject to recovery and Participant may
be required to repay to the Company all or a portion of any Award or payments received in connection with any Award hereunder. In the event that the Company determines to seek recovery with respect to an Award under this Agreement, the Company will
determine the appropriate means of recovery, which may vary, without limitation, between Participants or based on the nature of the applicable incentive compensation, and which may involve, without limitation, establishing a deferred repayment plan
or set off against current or future compensation otherwise payable to an affected Participant. The amount of any applicable repayment shall be determined without regard to income taxes paid by the Participant or by the Company on the
Participant&#146;s behalf in connection with such Award; <I>provided</I>, however, the Participant may be entitled, if allowed under applicable laws, rules, and regulations, to a deduction for the tax year within which such amounts are repaid, and
as a result, the timing of recovering the tax refund portion of such Award pursuant to the foregoing sentence shall (to the maximum extent practicable) be deferred to incorporate the timing of any such tax refund. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>APA Corporation </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Executive Compensation Clawback Policy </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>OUR POLICY </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has adopted this Policy for the
purpose of complying with the applicable recoupment provisions of the Dodd-Frank Wall Street Reform and Consumer Protection Act (the Dodd-Frank Act). This Policy applies to Incentive Compensation that is Received by a Covered Individual on or after
October&nbsp;2, 2023 (the Effective Date). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Recoupment Trigger </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If the Company is required to prepare an Accounting Restatement, then the Company shall recover, reasonably promptly from each Covered Individual, any
Erroneously Awarded Compensation that was Received by such Covered Individual during the Look-Back Period. Notwithstanding anything herein to the contrary, this Policy shall be deemed automatically and unilaterally amended to the minimum extent
necessary to comply with the applicable listing standards to which the Company is listed. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Committee may at any time suspend, amend, or terminate this
Policy to the minimum extent necessary to comply with applicable laws. The Committee has the sole discretion to interpret and enforce this Policy, which will be interpreted to be automatically amended to the minimum extent necessary to comply with
the provisions of the Dodd-Frank Act&#146;s clawback requirements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Enforcement and Impracticability </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Committee shall recover any Incentive Compensation in accordance with this Policy unless such recovery would be impracticable, as determined by the
Committee in accordance with Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10D-1</FONT> of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the Exchange Act), and the listing standards of the national securities exchange on which the Company&#146;s
securities are listed. To the extent the Committee determines to enforce recoupment, (i)&nbsp;the Committee shall provide the Covered Individual written notice of its intent to recoup Incentive Compensation under this Policy, along with a reasonable
timeline within which the Covered Individual must respond given all the applicable facts and circumstances, (ii)&nbsp;to the extent the Covered Individual does not intend to comply with such recoupment efforts, he or she must respond to the
Committee in writing detailing the reasons why <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-compliance</FONT> is warranted and such response must be provided to the Committee within fifteen (15)&nbsp;business days from the Covered Individual receiving the
Committee&#146;s initial notice, and (iii)&nbsp;if the Committee disagrees with the Covered Individual&#146;s assertions, then the Committee must respond to the Covered Individual in writing detailing such reasons within the fifteen
(15)&nbsp;business days immediately following its receipt of the Covered Individual&#146;s written response. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Means of Recovery </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to recovery of Erroneously Awarded Compensation and subject to the requirement that recovery be made reasonably promptly, the Committee will
determine the appropriate means of recovery, which may vary, without limitation, between Covered Individuals or based on the nature of the applicable Incentive Compensation, and which may involve, without limitation, establishing a deferred
repayment plan or set off against current or future compensation otherwise payable to the Covered Person. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery of Erroneously Awarded Compensation
will be made without regard to income taxes paid by the Covered Individual or by the Company on the Covered Individual&#146;s behalf in connection with such Erroneously Awarded Compensation; provided, however, the Covered Individual may be entitled
to a deduction (pursuant to the &#147;claim of right doctrine&#148; or Section&nbsp;1341 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended) for the tax year within which Erroneously Awarded Compensation is repaid, and as a result, the timing of
recovering the tax refund portion of Erroneously Awarded Compensation pursuant to the foregoing sentence shall (to the maximum extent practicable) be deferred to incorporate the timing of any such tax refund. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Page 18 of 21 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Compensation Not Covered by this Policy </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Policy does not apply to Incentive Compensation that was Received before the Effective Date and does not apply to Incentive Compensation that was Received
by a Covered Individual before becoming a Covered Individual. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>No Indemnification or Company-Paid Insurances </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company will not indemnify or reimburse any Covered Individual against or for the loss of Erroneously Awarded Compensation and will not pay or reimburse
any Covered Individual for the purchase of a third-party insurance policy to fund potential recovery obligations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Defined Terms </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Except as otherwise provided above, the following definitions apply to this Policy: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Accounting Restatement</B> means a requirement that the Company prepare an accounting restatement due to the material noncompliance of the Company with any
financial reporting requirement under the U.S. federal securities laws, including any required accounting restatement to correct an error in previously issued financial statements that is material to the previously issued financial statements, or
that would result in a material misstatement if the error were corrected in the current period or left uncorrected in the current period. Changes to the Company&#146;s financial statements that do not represent error corrections are not an
Accounting Restatement, including (i)&nbsp;retrospective application of a change in accounting principle, (ii)&nbsp;retrospective revision to reportable segment information due to a change in the structure of the Company&#146;s internal
organization, (iii)&nbsp;retrospective reclassification due to a discontinued operation, (iv)&nbsp;retrospective application of a change in reporting entity, such as from a reorganization of entities under common control, and (v)&nbsp;retrospective
revision for stock splits, reverse stock splits, stock dividends, or other changes in capital structure. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company</B> means APA Corporation, a Delaware
corporation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Covered Individual</B> means, whether former or current, the (i)&nbsp;named executive officers of the Company, (ii)&nbsp;each
&#147;executive officer&#148; of the Company (as such term is defined under Section&nbsp;16 of the Exchange Act), and (iii)&nbsp;any other officer of the Company or any of its subsidiaries that is designated by the Committee as being subject to this
Policy prior to the Company&#146;s discovery of the Accounting Restatement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Erroneously Awarded Compensation</B> means the amount of Incentive
Compensation that was Received that exceeds the amount of Incentive Compensation that otherwise would have been Received had the amount of Incentive Compensation been determined based on the restated Financial Reporting Measures, computed without
regard to any taxes paid by the Covered Individual, reduced by the amount of such Incentive Compensation that is recovered by the Company from such Covered Individual pursuant to Section&nbsp;304 of Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002, any other law, rule or
regulation, or any other means. For Incentive Compensation based on total shareholder return or Company stock price, where the amount of Erroneously Awarded Compensation is not subject to mathematical recalculation directly from the information in
an Accounting Restatement, the amount of Erroneously Awarded Compensation will be based on a reasonable estimate by the Committee of the effect of the Accounting Restatement on the stock price or total shareholder return upon which the Incentive
Compensation was Received. The Company will maintain documentation of the determination of that reasonable estimate and provide such documentation to Nasdaq if required. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Page 19 of 21 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Financial Reporting Measures</B> means (i)&nbsp;measures that are determined and presented in accordance
with the accounting principles used in preparing the Company&#146;s financial statements and any measures that are derived wholly or in part from such measures (whether or not such measures are presented within the Company&#146;s financial
statements or included in a filing made with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission), (ii) Company stock price, and (iii)&nbsp;Company total shareholder return. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Incentive Compensation</B> means the following compensation to the extent earned, paid, granted, or vested wholly (or in part) upon the attainment of any
Financial Reporting Measure of the Company: a Covered Individual&#146;s cash bonus awarded under the Company&#146;s annual incentive plan and any equity-based awards granted pursuant to the Company&#146;s long-term incentive plans (including cash or
stock dividends paid on such equity-based awards). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Look-Back Period</B> means the three completed fiscal years immediately preceding the earlier of
(i)&nbsp;the date the Company&#146;s Board of Directors (the Board), a committee of the Board, or the officer or officers of the Company authorized to take such action if Board action is not required, concludes, or reasonably should have concluded,
that the Company is required to prepare an Accounting Restatement or (ii)&nbsp;the date a court, regulator, or other legally authorized body directs the Company to prepare an Accounting Restatement. In addition, if there is a change in the
Company&#146;s fiscal year end, the Look-Back Period will also include any transition period to the extent required by Nasdaq Rule 5608. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Received</B>
means, with respect to Incentive Compensation of a Covered Individual, the fiscal year to which the Financial Reporting Measure is attained, irrespective of whether the Incentive Compensation is subject to additional time or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-financial</FONT> performance vesting conditions. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Page 20 of 21 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>APA Corporation </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Stock Option Award Agreement </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Stock
Option Award Agreement (this &#147;<B>Agreement</B>&#148;), dated as of the Grant Date set forth in the Grant Notice, is made between APA Corporation (together with its Affiliates, the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;) and the Participant set forth in the
Grant Notice. The Grant Notice is included in and made part of this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In this Agreement and the Grant Notice, unless the context otherwise
requires, words and expressions shall have the meanings given to them in the Plan except as herein defined. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Definitions </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Disability</B>&#148; or &#147;<B>Disabled</B>&#148; means the Participant is unable to engage in any substantial gainful activity by reason of any
medically determinable physical or mental impairment which can be expected to result in death or which has lasted or can be expected to last for a continuous period of not less than 12 months. Participant agrees that a final and binding
determination of &#147;Disability&#148; will be made by the Company&#146;s representative under the Company&#146;s group long-term disability plan or any successor thereto or, if there is no such representative and there is a dispute as to the
determination of &#147;Disability,&#148; it will be decided in a court of law in Harris County, Texas. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Grant Notice</B>&#148; means the separate
notice, attached as Schedule A hereto, given to the Participant specifying the number of Shares underlying the Option granted to the Participant (the &#147;<B>Grant</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Involuntary Termination</B>&#148; means the termination of employment of the Participant by the Company or its successor or an applicable Affiliate
for any reason on or after a Change of Control; <I>provided</I>, that the termination does not result from an act of the Participant that (a)&nbsp;constitutes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">common-law</FONT> fraud, a felony, or a gross malfeasance
of duty and (b)&nbsp;is materially detrimental to the best interests of the Company or its successor; <I>provided</I> that, notwithstanding anything else in this Agreement to the contrary, an Involuntary Termination shall not be deemed to occur
solely because a Participant transfers employment from the Company to an Affiliate, from an Affiliate to the Company, or from one Affiliate to another Affiliate. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Plan</B>&#148; means the APA Corporation 2016 Omnibus Compensation Plan, as amended. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Retirement</B>&#148; means, with respect to a Participant and for purposes of this Agreement, the date the Participant terminates employment with the
Company after (a)&nbsp;attaining age 60 or (b)&nbsp;attaining age 55 and a certain combination of age and Years of Service set forth in the Matrix in Exhibit A attached hereto. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Years of Service</B>&#148; means the total number of months from the Participant&#146;s date of hire by the Company or the Affiliates to the date of
termination of employment, plus any months required to be recognized under an appropriate acquisition agreement, divided by 12. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;<B>Voluntary
Termination with Cause</B>&#148; occurs upon a Participant&#146;s separation from service of his or her own volition and one or more of the following conditions occurs without the Participant&#146;s consent on or after a Change of Control: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>(a)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material diminution in the Participant&#146;s base compensation, compared to his or her rate of base
compensation on the date of the Change of Control. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>(b)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material diminution in the Participant&#146;s authority, duties, or responsibilities.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>(c)</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">There is a material diminution in the authority, duties, or responsibilities of the Participant&#146;s
supervisor, such as a requirement that the Participant (or his or her supervisor) report to a corporate officer or employee instead of reporting directly to the board of directors. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Page 3 of 10 </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

including, for example the assignment of the Participant to a regular workplace that is more than 50 miles from his or her regular workplace on the date of the Change of Control. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Participant must notify the Company of the existence of one or more adverse conditions specified in clauses (a)&nbsp;through (e) above within 90 days of
the initial existence of the adverse condition. The notice must be provided in writing to the Company or its successor, attention: Head of Human Resources. The notice may be provided by personal delivery or it may be sent by email, inter-office
mail, regular mail (including certified), fax, or any similar method. The Company&#146;s Head of Human Resources or his or her delegate shall acknowledge receipt of the notice within 5 business days; the acknowledgement shall be sent to the
Participant by certified mail. Notwithstanding the foregoing provisions of this definition, if the Company remedies the adverse condition within 30 days of being notified of the adverse condition, no Voluntary Termination with Cause shall occur.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Terms </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Grant of the Option</B>. Subject to the provisions of this Agreement and the provisions of the Plan and
Grant Notice, the Company hereby grants to the Participant, pursuant to the Plan, the right and option (the &#147;<B>Option</B>&#148;) to purchase all or any part of the number of shares of $0.625 par value common stock of the Company
(&#147;<B>Shares</B>&#148;) set forth in the Grant Notice at the Option Price per Share and on the other terms as set forth in the Grant Notice. The Option is intended to be a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Qualified</FONT> Stock Option.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

personal, certified, or cashier&#146;s check payable in U.S. dollars sent or delivered to Fidelity; (iii)&nbsp;by delivery to Fidelity of certificates representing a number of Shares then owned by the Participant having an aggregate Fair Market
Value at the Exercise Date equal to the aggregate Option Price; (iv)&nbsp;by certification or attestation to Fidelity of the Participant&#146;s ownership as of the Exercise Date of a number of Shares having an aggregate Fair Market Value at the
Exercise Date not greater than the aggregate Option Price; (v)&nbsp;by delivery to Fidelity of a properly executed written notice of exercise together with irrevocable instructions to a broker to promptly deliver to the Company, by wire transfer or
check as provided in clause (i)&nbsp;or (ii) of this section 3(b), the amount of the proceeds of the sale of all or a portion of the Shares as to which the Option is so exercised or of a loan from the broker to the Participant necessary to pay the
aggregate Option Price; or (vi)&nbsp;by a combination of the consideration provided for in the foregoing clauses (i), (ii), (iii), (iv), and (v). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>Disclosure of Confidential Information</I></B>. The Participant divulges any <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-public,</FONT> confidential or proprietary information of the Company, but excluding information that (i)&nbsp;becomes generally available to the public other than as a result of the Participant&#146;s public use,
disclosure, or fault or (ii)&nbsp;becomes available to the Participant on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-confidential</FONT> basis after the Participant&#146;s employment termination date from a source other than the Company prior to the
public use or disclosure by the Participant, <I>provided</I> that such source is not bound by a confidentiality agreement or otherwise prohibited from transmitting the information by contractual, legal, or fiduciary obligation.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

affiliated with, participates or engages in, or becomes employed by any business that is competitive with the Company, wherever from time to time conducted throughout the world, including situations where the Participant solicits or participates in
